Lecture 12: Preparing journal artical with papaja

48 6.2 问卷数据

6.2.2 操作步骤 | Step4: 计算所需变量[mutate]

# 计算ALEX
df1 <- mutate(df1, 
              ALEX = rowSums(select(df1, starts_with("ALEX"))))

# 查看数据
